This also motivates the child to want to get higher awards and better marks.\r\n\r\nThere are 41 subtopics categorized as follows:\r\n\r\nNumbers\r\n\r\n1.\tWrite\r\n2.\tPlace Value\r\n3.\tRounding\r\n4.\tCompare\r\n5.\tRoman Numerals\r\n6.\tSpecial Numbers\r\n\r\nCalculations\r\n\r\n7.\tAddition\r\n8.\tSubtraction\r\n9.\tMultiplication\r\n10.\tDivision\r\n11.\tSolve Problems\r\n\r\nFractions\r\n\r\n12.\t Simplify\r\n13.\tAddition\r\n14.\tSubtraction\r\n15.\tMultiplication\r\n16.\tDivision\r\n17.\tConvert\r\n18.\tSolve Problems\r\n\r\nDecimals\r\n\r\n19.\t Addition\r\n20.\t Subtraction\r\n21.\tDivision\r\n22.\t Multiplication\r\n23.\t Rounding\r\n24.\t Compare\r\n25.\t Solve Problems\r\n\r\nMeasurements\r\n\r\n26.\t Length Mass and Volume\r\n27.\t Area and Perimeter \r\n28.\t Time\r\n29.\t Money\r\n30.\t Solve Problems\r\n\r\nGeometry\r\n\r\n31.\t 3D Shapes and Nets\r\n32.\t Angles\r\n33.\t Coordinates\r\n34.\t Reflection\r\n\r\nStatistics\r\n\r\n35.\tCharts\r\n36.\tMean, Mode and Range\r\n37.\tProbability\r\n38.\tRatio and Proportion\r\n\r\nAlgebra\r\n\r\n39.\tFormula\r\n40.\tMissing Numbers\r\n41.\tSequences\r\n\r\nTEST RESULTS\r\n\r\nOn the completion of each test the user is given a summary of questions answered correctly and incorrectly, the percentage achieved in the test and the time taken on each test.  Each test displays the actual percentage scored and also shows the time that the test took. This has been invaluable for top performing children who have achieved diamond status as they can improve on the time the tests are taking them. Every question can be reviewed and all questions have an answer.\r\n\r\nEND OF YEAR TEST\r\n\r\nAfter your child has practiced all the subtopics, they can take an end of year test with 50 questions. The end of year test has randomly selected questions from each topic.
